Assessment (8)

Assessment Assess_Cadence_1
Mix of short declaratives ('Nothing built.', 'The difference is who pays and who drives.') and longer analytical sentences. Table and bullet structures create visual rhythm. Cadence is functional rather than rhetorical — appropriate for mem
Assessment Assess_Flow_1
Strong flow: Current Capability → Gap Analysis → Backlog Alignment → Two GTM Motions → Tension → Unifying Insight → Prioritization. Each section builds on the prior. Transitions are implicit (section headers) rather than explicit connective
Assessment Assess_Novelty_1
High novelty in the core insight (enterprise engagement = Salon primitive). Taxonomy terms (Solo/Parallel/Hub/Salon/Teams) are original vocabulary. Some backlog section language is generic ('heavily weighted toward'). The 'Unifying Insight'
Assessment Assess_Phrasing_1
Characteristic phrasing includes 'The difference is who pays and who drives' and 'Nothing built.' — short, declarative, confident. Taxonomy terms (Solo/Salon/Teams) function as controlled vocabulary. Some generic phrasing in backlog section
Assessment Assess_Register_1
Strong register fit for internal strategic memo. Neutral-to-formal, analytical, no hype. Active voice dominant. Slight informality in parenthetical asides ('Tony: ...') is appropriate for founder-AI context. Supporting obs: narr:StyleObs_9.
Assessment Assess_Resonance_1
Resonance achieved primarily through the structural analogy (Pilot=Salon, Full engagement=Teams, Retainer=Parallel) and the quoted external voice (Tony). Gap analysis table adds concrete grounding. No narrative story arc or emblematic custo
Assessment Assess_StrategicAlignment_1
Exceptionally strong strategic alignment. Document explicitly maps product capability to use-case taxonomy, backlog to GTM motions, and resolves apparent tension via the 'Unifying Insight' analogy. Directly addresses mission (collective mem
Assessment Assess_Tailoring_1
Well-tailored to the founder-AI coworker audience: assumes shared context (taxonomy defined in related doc, backlog task IDs referenced), uses internal shorthand (msg/*, task-081), and addresses Scarlet's specific decision context. Would sc

WhatIsIt (1)

WhatIsIt WhatIsIt_SMSProduct
SMS-first collective memory: text a number, state your topic, name your contacts. The AI interviews everyone asynchronously, synthesizes perspectives, surfaces contradictions with provenance, and notifies you when consensus forms or shifts.
Materialized from aswritten's own knowledge graph — every page is generated from witnessed, dated, attributed organizational discourse. Names of customers and collaborators are anonymized; the reasoning is real. Install it in your own AI: perspective id customer-architecture-demo-enterprise-a21e.
